        return load

class op646_loop_body:
    var_ranges = {p0: 512, p1: 512, p2: 784}
    index0 = 401408*p0 + p1 + 512*p2
    index1 = 401408*p0 + 784*p1 + p2
    def body(self, ops):
        get_index = self.get_index('index0')
        load = ops.load('buf547', get_index)
        get_index_1 = self.get_index('index0')
        load_1 = ops.load('buf606', get_index_1)
        add = ops.add(load, load_1)
        get_index_2 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_2 = ops.load('buf612', get_index_2)
        to_dtype = ops.to_dtype(load_2, torch.bfloat16, src_dtype = torch.int8)
        mul = ops.mul(add, to_dtype)
        get_index_3 = self.get_index('index0')
        load_3 = ops.load('buf671', get_index_3)
        add_1 = ops.add(mul, load_3)
